***завидовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завидовать.html>зави́довать</a> (3330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завидовать.html>зави́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavídovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позавидовать.html>позави́довать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to envy, to be envious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завидный.html>зави́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavídnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">завидущий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaviduščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***зависать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависать.html>зависа́ть</a> (27488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависать.html>зависа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hover <i>(above)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be taken up <i>(with)</i>, to get a bee in one's bonnet <i>(about)</i></li></ol>

***зависеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависеть.html>зави́сеть</a> (1569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висеть.html>висе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">visétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависеть.html>зави́сеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavísetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>no perfective form</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to depend (on), to rely (on) - (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бществе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> како́й-то <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зависеть.html>зави́сим</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́нов</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vse my živjóm v óbščestve i v kakój-to stépeni <b>zavísim</b> ot jevó zakónov.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We all live in the society and to some extent <b>depend</b> on its laws.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ра</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зависеть.html>зави́сит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́чества</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Cená továra <b>zavísit</b> ot jevó káčestva.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The price of the commodity <b>depends</b> on its quality.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***зависнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́снуть</a> (14192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виснуть.html>ви́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavísnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависать.html>зависа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hover <i>(above)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kompʹjútɛr <b>zavís</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the computer hung</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be taken up <i>(with)</i>, to get a bee in one's bonnet <i>(about)</i></li></ol>

</ul></li>


</ol>

***завитушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завитушка.html>завиту́шка</a> (25266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зави́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Appearance of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-т-</span> is unexpected but also found in other derivatives of the same verb.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завитушка.html>завиту́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavitúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завитушка.html>завиту́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завитушка.html>завиту́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завитушка.html>завиту́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ringlet, lock <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hair</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>flourish, twirl, whorl, curl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rhetorical flourish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">artsy, complex figure of speech</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***завладеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завладеть.html>завладе́ть</a> (9877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владеть.html>владе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vladétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завладеть.html>завладе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavladétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">завладева́ть</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to take possession <i>(of)</i>, to seize</li>
<li>to capture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завладеть.html>завладе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavladétʹ</b> umámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rule the minds</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завладеть.html>завладе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavladétʹ</b> vnimánijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grip someone's attention</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a> (875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>factory, plant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водочный.html>во́дочный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vódočnyj <b>zavód</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">vodka <b>distillery</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kónskij <b>zavód</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stud <b>farm</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">рыбово́дный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rybovódnyj <b>zavód</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fish <b>farm</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>winding mechanism</li>
<li>winding up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>Для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришло́сь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>ма́стера</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dlja <b>zavóda</b> starínnyx časóv prišlósʹ výzvatʹ mástera.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We had to call a professional to <b>wind up</b> the antique clock.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ть</a> (6747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завести.html>завести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take, to bring, to lead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>тупи́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavodítʹ</b> v tupík</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead up a blind alley</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get, to procure, to acquire, to buy</li>
<li>to establish, to set up, to found</li>
<li>to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводить.html>заводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavodítʹ</b> razgovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start a conversation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(a habit, friendship)</i> to form, to contract</li>
<li>to start <i>(a motor)</i>, to wind up <i>(clock)</i></li>
<li>to get somebody worked up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заводи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavodítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завестись.html>завести́сь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vesti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведение.html>заведе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavedénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***заводиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заводи́ться</a> (11008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водиться.html>води́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заводи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завестись.html>завести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be acquired <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, by someone; normally expressed in English in the active voice</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заво́дятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>zavódjatsja</b> dénʹgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he's is getting money (to spend)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">money <b>is being acquired</b> by him</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заво́дятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзья́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tam u menjá <b>zavódjatsja</b> nóvyje druzʹjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am getting/meeting/acquiring new friends there</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">new friends <b>are being acquired</b> by me there</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to infest <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, someone, or + location, somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́ром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ме</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заво́дятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v stárom dóme <b>zavódjatsja</b> mýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mice <b>are infesting</b> the old house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заво́дятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вша.html>вши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nejó <b>zavódjatsja</b> vši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she's becoming infested with lice</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">lice <b>are infesting</b> her</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be wound up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a mechanism or clock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; to start <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a car or motor</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get worked up, to be turned on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводиться.html>заводи́сь</a></b> и́з-за <a href = vnd.unilang:пустяк.html>пустяка́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>zavodísʹ</b> íz-za pustjaká!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't get all <b>worked up</b> over nothing!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завести.html>завести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Note the construction of the verb in the first definition and corresponding examples. What is typically rendered as the subject in English is in Russian specified using <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, normally preceding the verb, while the verb agrees with what is, from the English perspective, the object.</li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заводной.html>заводно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavodnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clockwork, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wind-up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводной.html>заводна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игрушка.html>игру́шка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavodnája</b> igrúška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">clockwork toy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заводной.html>заводна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукоятка.html>рукоя́тка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavodnája</b> rukojátka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starting crank/handle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lively, quick-moving, full of pep</li></ol>
